--mapping procedure
create or replace PROCEDURE         "BRF1_MAPPING_PROCEDURE" ( REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2) 
IS 

  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 


BEGIN 


UPDATE BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET nre_status='N' WHERE country_of_incorp IN ('AE','AE*','UAE') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;
COMMIT;

UPDATE BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET nre_status='Y' WHERE country_of_incorp NOT IN ('AE','AE*','UAE') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;
COMMIT;



--1.1	Cash in hand 


UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW102' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Cash in hand'
WHERE  GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE IN ('26671','21101') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE AND SOL_ID IN ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008');
COMMIT;

--1.2	Statutory reserve with CB


UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW103' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Statutory reserve with CB'
WHERE  GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE IN ('22203') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE AND (FORACID LIKE '%1622203003%') AND SOL_ID IN ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008');

COMMIT;

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW103' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Statutory reserve with CB'
WHERE   FORACID IN ('A22010043','A22022019') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

COMMIT;

--1.3	Free deposits (30% of Dirham lending to non residents)--NIL

--1.4	Other balances

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW105' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Other balances'
WHERE   FORACID IN ('A22022020') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

COMMIT;

--1.5.1	Repoed to UAE Central Bank (gross)
--1.5.2	Others- unencumbered

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW108' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Others- unencumbered'
WHERE   FORACID IN ('A22022018') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

COMMIT;

--2.1	Due from Head Office of foreign banks & their banking subs.

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW110' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='2.1',nre_status='Y'
WHERE   FORACID IN ('A61111001','A61111002','A61111003','A61111004','A61150000')AND ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC<0  AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

COMMIT;

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW110' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='2.1',nre_status='Y'
WHERE   FORACID IN ('A61160000') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

COMMIT;

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW110' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='2.1',nre_status='Y'
WHERE  GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE IN ('31104') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE AND FORACID IN ('90010200012605','90010200012604','90010200018894') AND SOL_ID IN ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008') AND ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC<0;

COMMIT;

--2.2	Due from overseas BR of national banks/ Banking Subs.-NIL
--2.3	Bills discounted on own branches, subsidiaries,etc  without recourse -NIL

--3.1	Money at call and short notice, placements on demand and remaining balances---NEED CLARIFICATIION

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW114' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='3.1',nre_status='Y'
WHERE   FORACID IN ('A22010009', 'A22010004', 'A22010022', 'A22010029', 'A22010032', 'A22010040', 'A22010046', 'A22010054', 'A22010059', 
'A22010060', 'A22010061', 'A22010078', 'A22010081') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE AND ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC<0;	

COMMIT;


--3.2	Interbank placements-NEED CLARIFICATION

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW115' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Interbank placements',nre_status='N'
WHERE  FORACID IN ('A21012202', 'A22022009', 'A22022008') AND acct_crncy_code='AED' AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;	

COMMIT;


UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW115' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Interbank placements',nre_status='Y'
WHERE  FORACID IN ('A21012202', 'A22022009', 'A22022008')  AND acct_crncy_code NOT IN ('AED') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;	

COMMIT;


--3.3	Other term placements (loans)

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW116' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Other term placements (loans)',nre_status='Y'
WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE NOT IN ('44101', '44102','44103', '44104', '44105', '44106', '44107', '44108', '44109', '44110', '44111', '44112', 
'44113', '44114', '44115', '44116', '44199','44201', '44202', '44203', '44204', '44205', '44206', '44207', '44208', '44209', '44210', '44211', 
'44212', '44213', '44214', '44215', '44216', '44217', '44299', '71005', 'HUFJT', 'INDL','INDL ', 'INDVF', 'INDVM', 'NREIN', 'RESIN','WPS') and 
legal_entity_type not in('GOVTF','CGOVB','CB','GOVT','GOVTL','GOVTE','PSENO','PSEN','PSEC','PSECO')
and purpose_of_advn  in ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9007','9009','9034','9035','9036','9037') AND ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC<0 AND SOL_ID IN ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

COMMIT;

--3.4	Cheques in the course of collection
--3.5	Banks' bills purchased  without recourse
--3.6	Lending covered by repurchase agreements



--4.2	Placements
--4.3	Lending covered by repurchase agreements
--	INVESTMENTS AND FINANCIAL ASSETS-BRF 5
--5.1	Trading Book Securities (market value) 
--5.1.1	Debt securities
--5.1.2	Equities
--5.1.3	Commodities

--4.1	NBFI-Loans and advances

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW121' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='NBFI'
WHERE legal_entity_type  IN ('NBFC','MXC','MXC  ','NBFC ') 
AND SOL_ID IN ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008') AND ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC<0 AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

COMMIT;

--5.2	Banking Book-5.2.1	Available for sale--5.2.1.1	Debt securities-NEED CLARIFICATION

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW131' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Debt securities'
WHERE   FORACID IN ('A31013016', 'A31031210', 'A34022024', 'A34022200', 'A66044200') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;
COMMIT;

--5.2.1.2	Equities

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW132' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Equities',nre_status='Y'
WHERE   FORACID IN ('A33012100') 
AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

COMMIT;

--5.2.2	Held to maturity (amortised cost)
--	OTHER INVESTMENTS - BRF 5
--6.1	Investment in subsidiaries (Cost or fair value)
--6.2	Investment in affiliates (Cost or fair value)
	--TRADE BILLS DISCOUNTED
--7.1	TRADE BILLS DISCOUNTED- Gov & Public Sector
--7.1.1	Inland trade bills/ PDCs
--7.1.2	Foreign trade bills (Import and export)

--7.2	TRADE BILLS DISCOUNTED- Private-7.2.1	Inland trade bills/ PDCs- NEED CLARIFICATION HAVING EXTRA GLSH CODE IN HEENA LOGIC

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW142' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Inland trade bills/ PDCs'
WHERE constitution_code not in ('44101', '44102',
'44103', '44104', '44105', '44106', '44107', '44108', '44109', '44110', '44111', '44112', '44113', '44114', '44115', '44116', '44199',
'44201', '44202', '44203', '44204', '44205', '44206', '44207', '44208', '44209', '44210', '44211', '44212', '44213', '44214', '44215', 
'44216', '44217', '44299', '71005', 'HUFJT', 'INDL','INDL ', 'INDVM', 'NREIN', 'RESIN','WPS') and 
legal_entity_type not in('GOVTF','CGOVB','CB','GOVT','GOVTL','GOVTE','PSENO','PSEN','PSEC','PSECO','NBFC','MXC','MXC  ','NBFC ')
and purpose_of_advn not in ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9007','9009','9034','9035','9036','9037')
and GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE  in('24101','24102','24116','24117','24122','24146') AND ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC<0 AND SOL_ID IN ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

COMMIT;

UPDATE  BRF1_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF1', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW142' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='Inland trade bills/ PDCs'
WHERE foracid in ('90010800000206') AND ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC<0 AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

---detail procedure
create or replace PROCEDURE         "BRF1_DETAIL_PROCEDURE" (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
   v_report_date   date := to_date (report_date, 'DD-MM-YYYY');
BEGIN


Delete from BRF1_DETAILTABLE where REPORT_DATE = '30-jun-2023';
Commit;

--DEVELOPED BY -SURIYA K
--DATE         - 2/6/2023
------INSERT QUERY----
----INSERT QUERY----
insert into brf1_detailtable
(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,ACCT_NAME,FORACID,ACID,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,CUST_ID,NRE_FLG,REMARKS,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1,REPORT_DATE,REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,SOL_ID)
select ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,ACCT_NAME,FORACID,ACID,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,CUST_ID,NRE_STATUS,REMARKS,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1,REPORT_DATE,REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,SOL_ID from brf1_mapping_table 
where report_date='30-JUN-2023' and report_label_1 is not null;



COMMIT;
END;

delete from BRF1_SUMMARYTABLE where report_date =V_REPORT_DATE;

SELECT round(sum(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC)/1000) INTO V_R2_AMOUNT_AED_RESIDENT  FROM BRF1_DETAILTABLE   
WHERE  REPORT_DATE =V_REPORT_DATE AND ACCT_CRNCY_CODE ='AED' AND REPORT_LABEL_1= 'ROW102' AND nvl(NRE_FLG ,'N') ='N';

V_R2_AMOUNT_AED_RESIDENT:=abs(V_R2_AMOUNT_AED_RESIDENT);

SELECT round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) INTO V_R2_AMOUNT_FCY_RESIDENT  FROM BRF1_DETAILTABLE   
WHERE  REPORT_DATE =V_REPORT_DATE AND ACCT_CRNCY_CODE  <> 'AED' AND REPORT_LABEL_1= 'ROW102' AND nvl(NRE_FLG ,'N') ='N';


SELECT round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) INTO V_R2_AMOUNT_AED_NON_RESIDENT  FROM BRF1_DETAILTABLE   
WHERE  REPORT_DATE =V_REPORT_DATE AND ACCT_CRNCY_CODE ='AED' AND REPORT_LABEL_1= 'ROW102' AND nvl(NRE_FLG ,'N') ='Y';

SELECT round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) INTO V_R2_AMOUNT_FCY_NON_RESIDENT  FROM BRF1_DETAILTABLE   
WHERE  REPORT_DATE =V_REPORT_DATE AND ACCT_CRNCY_CODE  <> 'AED' AND REPORT_LABEL_1= 'ROW102' AND nvl(NRE_FLG ,'N') ='Y';
